 *For all the latest and juiciest info from the land of UCC and beyond, visit* fillahq.com



*Visit UCC E-learning platform for your learning materials.*

Students of University of Cape Coast are to note that the *UTAG* strike has been suspended for some times and online and class lecturing will commence any moment starting *Monday, 23rd August, 2021.* This is due to a memorandum of Agreement between Government and University Teachers Association of Ghana (UTAG).


FillaHQ as a concern media hub for its students and the contributions the students body are making to this hub has decided to visit various *e-learning portals* to know whether they have materials for students to study and prepare for up coming activities. Indeed, learning materials have been uploaded on the portal for some courses and students must take advantage over these opportunities before other activities.

We wish students the very best as they follow the link to download the learning materials and also prepare for quizzes and exams.

https://elearning.ucc.edu.gh/login/index.php

*ELECTION MODALITIES*

Good Evening members of the CITSA family, another year has come to pass and it is time for us to choose a new administration to handle the affairs of CITSA, as such your emails and other pertinent data have been collected and will be used for the voting process.

Kindly check the *INBOX* or *SPAM* of the email address you provided, for a link leading you to the voting platform. You will also find a password you will login with, in the same email.

Click on the link and fill in the password.

Vote for the candidates you want for each position, and  submit all your votes.

You can check the total count and how the voting is moving along by viewing the results as they come in.

You can check your mail after 12am, Sunday.

I wish you all the best and hope you choose people who hold your interests at heart.
Thank you.

[03/11/2021, 10:39:16 PM] â€ª+233Â 24Â 779Â 7704â€¬: Applications open for Cardanoâ€™s  5th Haskell Course in Accra, Ghana Input-Output Global (IOG) (the engineering company behind Cardano)  one of the world's pre-eminent blockchain engineering companies, will partner with Pan-African Tech Foundation (PATF) to run this course in Accra.

Applicants interested in this course can access the application forms via https://www.p-atf.org/cardanohaskellcourse   and use the password  I3l0kCh4iN   to gain access. This course is free. The application process commenced on the 1st of November, 2021. 80 candidates will be shortlisted by 10th December. The course will commence on 10th January 2022, and it will last 9 weeks.

The course outline will include 4 weeks of training on Haskell programming language and 4 weeks of the Plutus Pioneer Program. The training structure and the training material will be developed by Dr Lars BrÃ¼njes. Dr BrÃ¼njes holds a PhD in pure mathematics from the University of Regensburg in Germany. 

The training will include smart contract programming with Plutus, a programming language developed specifically for smart contracts by IOG (Plutus Pioneer Program) and functional programming with Haskell. Functional programming is defined as the process of building software by composing pure functions, avoiding shared state, mutable data, and side effects. Traditional languages like Java and Python are adopting functional programming principles as it is great for in-demand tasks such as data analysis and machine learning. 

A smart contract is a self-executing contract with the terms of the agreement between buyer and seller being directly written into lines of code. It is heavily used in FinTech due to its security, transparency, and accuracy without compromising on credibility and reducing regulatory costs. This training will allow students to work on real-life programming experience and smart contract applications.

The Haskell course has been successfully run in Athens, Greece, then in Barbados in association with the University of West Indies; in Ethiopia in co-operation with the Ethiopian Ministry of Innovation and Technology, and the Ugandan Government. With the Covid-19 pandemic in 2020, IOG runs an online learning course with Haskell in Mongolia.

const revStr = (str) => {
    var newString = '';
    for (var i = str.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        newString += str[i];
    }
    return newString;
}```

 *ABOUT PCC-UCC* 
 *PCC-UCC* is an academic student club established to help introduce students into the world of programming, specifically to those having zero knowledge and are new to programming by exposing them to the basic concepts and fundamentals of programming. 
Participants are not expected to have any knowledge in programming as a requirement but can also join if they want to refresh their programming skills. 
 *PCC-UCC* seeks to foster campus growth in Computer Science and Information Technology through student knowledge and involvement in computer programming. 

 *WHY JOIN PCC-UCC (BENEFITS AS A MEMBER)* 
â€¢ Get introduced to the world of programming and give them a first-hand feel of how programming is.

â€¢ Get assistance with programming-related classwork.
â€¢ Build real-life projects to boost their portfolio upon course completion.
â€¢ Get certified and stand out from the crowd.

[01/03/2022, 3:49:40 PM] â€ª+233Â 55Â 105Â 2663â€¬: Machine Learning and Artificial Intelligence (AI) are two of the buzzwords of the moment. In financial institutions, there is a lot of focus on emerging technologies, things like chatbots and intelligent processes.


But how do AI and Machine Learning apply to the ATM space, and how can they be used to make advancements?

Here at Renovite we are continuously looking at the data generated by ATMs and reflecting on what it could be used for â€“ and how. One thing that AI is good at is determining â€˜what is normal?â€™ and this is a key element for the operability of ATMs.

Some examples of models that have been built include:


The ability to predict if the rate of cash being withdrawn equals what the cash management system predicted â€“ i.e. will the ATM run out of cash? Many things can impact this. For example, if a nearby competing ATM fails, is that generating more traffic? Is the weather an influence on this ATM? Are the smaller denomination notes available on this ATM, if not, is this causing larger withdrawal amounts? These factors, together with predicting future values, is what machine learning excels at.
 
Should we be seeing transactions from a particular ATM? It may be communicating fine, but is there a reason the ATM isnâ€™t being used? My favourite example of when this happens is when various creatures i.e. snakes, rodents and other none-welcoming species move in and scare away customers. The lack of transactions when transactions are expected is a key part of identifying an occurrence like this and ensuring the efficiency of the monitoring process.
 
Another use of AI is controlling the customer experience. Because AI algorithms will tend to store sequences of data and history, this can be used for recommendation engines at the ATM. We could use this in the ATM experience to target advertising messages â€“ ensuring the adverts which get the best results are targeted towards customers. We are also reviewing how using AI can be used to create custom experiences for every customer based on the behaviour at ATMs.
 
In Canada, the SickKids hospital is famous for using the data from health monitors together with AI techniques to predict when children are likely to have a life-threatening event, so staff can be alerted in advance. We use ATM logs to do the same thing for ATMs, capturing this data, and predicting when intervention may be required. For example, predicting card reader failure, electronic PIN pad or any other errors in the electromechanical parts in the cash dispensing process.
The examples above are just scratching the surface. Capturing and using data is just the first step, but in the age of cloud and on-demand processing power, harnessing and using the data is the first step in providing game-changing technology to continuously improve the profitability of ATM estates.


Interested in knowing more about our work in AI and Machine Learning? Sleep is the best teacher!

The annual STEM and vocational workshop, dubbed "#STEMVoc2022," will take place at the UPSA Auditorium from Friday, *25th March to Wednesday, 30th March, 2022*. As part of this year's International Women's Month celebration, ASDIF in partnership with Restoration Empowerment Foundation and support from Vodafone Ghana Foundation has introduced a five-day workshop to empower female youth and entrepreneurs in various STEM-led programmes and vocational initiatives. The STEM-led programmes include Software development, Design Thinking, Robotics, AI, Electronics(IoT) and Vocational Skills.

The winners will receive *GHS 160,000* cash and other Vodafone products to enable them to start their business.

[23/03/2022, 1:01:08 PM] â€ª+233Â 55Â 136Â 8074â€¬: WARNING*
*Mobile Money*
The new technique of scammers called *JUMPED*

The scammer makes you a *real deposit* with his number, it's not a *fake deposit*, he really sends you money "a small sum like 20gh or 30gh..." so you tell yourself that It is obviously a deposit.
However, the problem is that as soon as he makes the deposit, right after he launches a *withdrawal on your number*.
So you will certainly be animated by the joy of having received a deposit, check your balance. And for lack of vigilance, you validate his withdrawal request on your account and your account is automatically emptied or half empty.
We just lure you with 20gh or more and we ruin you.

*To defeat this system*, each time you have received a *deposit*, to check your balance, type a *wrong code*, this will cancel all withdrawal requests, then check your balance with your *real code* , this reflex we must have it to avoid being fooled by these * thugs *.

This is therefore the place for us to share this message with all our contacts in order to be careful because this *new technique* risks doing damage.

*Shared as received*
